### `player.dta`

**NOTE**: Since Doom WAD files store data sequentially, redundant file
names are distinguished by character name. For development reasons, these
are listed in terms of the original cast of players from Sonic Robo Blast 2
(SRB2).  The following table shows the associative relationships between
SRB2 and TC characters:

| SRB2 character | TC character |
|================|==============|
| sonic          | elise        |
| tails          | kleene       |
| knuckles       | babel        |
| amy            | alex         |
| fang           | patsy        |
| metalsonic     | mara         |
